      * USER: Process Data record

     C                     END                             *FI
      * Select Kill Date
      * CASE:

      *   |- c2    : DB1.TH Kill Date GT PAR.Date To   USR
      *   '-

     C                     MOVEL'N'       W0RSL            *Record selecte

     C           WAUSST    OREQ '2'
     C           WAUSST    OREQ '3'
      * Rtv Held Over KillDt  RT - Tattoo Header  * 
     C                     EXSR SCRVGN

      * Record already deleted

      * Record not found label: LBL002.

     C                     MOVEL'Y2U0009' ZAMSID
     C                     MOVEL'Y2USRMSG'ZAMSGF
     C                     MOVELMD0009    ZAMSDA           Message data
     C                     EXSR ZASNMS

     C                     ENDIF

      * Record locked

      * Rtv Balance Info      RT - Tattoo Header  * 
      *================================================================
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    W0RTN   7
      * USER: Initialize routine
      * PAR = CON By name
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    YL0141           TH PHA Add Type
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    YL0142           TH PHA Average
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    YL0143           TH PHA Add Reas
      * Define keylist
     C           KRSSQ     KLIST
     C                     KFLD           WCHMNB           BOH Company Num
     C                     KFLD           WCBNNB           BOH Buy Order N
     C                     KFLD           WCBONB           BOL Load Number
     C                     KFLD           WCCVNB           TH Tattoo Numbe
     C                     KFLD           WCB0DT           TH Kill Date
      * Setup key
     C                     Z-ADDWAHMNB    WCHMNB           BOH Company Num
     C                     Z-ADDWABNNB    WCBNNB           BOH Buy Order N
     C                     Z-ADDWABONB    WCBONB           BOL Load Number
     C                     Z-ADDWACVNB    WCCVNB           TH Tattoo Numbe
     C                     Z-ADDWAB0DT    WCB0DT           TH Kill Date
      * Establish starting position
     C           KRSSQ     CHAIN@A1CPC4              90    *
      * Data record not found
     C   90                MOVEL'PRK0061' W0RTN   7
     C           *IN90     IFEQ '0'
      * USER: Process Data record
      * PAR = DB1 By name
     C                     MOVELWCOQET    YL0141           TH PHA Add Type
     C                     MOVELWCURST    YL0142           TH PHA Average
     C                     MOVELWCUSST    YL0143           TH PHA Add Reas
     C                     ENDIF

     CSR         SRRVGN    BEGSR
      *================================================================
      * Rtv GA Prod Hist Avgs RT - Producer History WKLY  * 
      *================================================================
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    W0RTN   7
      * USER: Initialize routine
      * PAR = CON By name
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    YL0145           PH Summary Type
     C                     Z-ADD*ZERO     YL0146           PH GA Avg Live
     C                     Z-ADD*ZERO     YL0147           PH GA Adjusted
     C                     Z-ADD*ZERO     YL0148           PH GA Avg Lean%
     C                     Z-ADD*ZERO     YL0149           PH GA Avg Backf
     C                     Z-ADD*ZERO     YL0150           PH GA Avg Loin
     C                     Z-ADD*ZERO     YL0151           PH GA Avg Light
     C                     Z-ADD*ZERO     YL0152           PH GA Lean Prm
     C                     Z-ADD*ZERO     YL0153           PH GA Avg Srt D
     C                     MOVEL*BLANK    YL0154           History Avail S
     C                     MOVEL'N'       YL0154           History Avail S
     C                     MOVEL'Y'       YL0155           First Time Flag
      * Declare restrictor key work fields
     C           *LIKE     DEFN WGY3A1    WQSR01           PH Company Numb
     C           *LIKE     DEFN WGABCD    WQSR02           PD Producer Cod
      * Define keylist
     C           KPSSR     KLIST
     C                     KFLD           WQSR01           PH Company Numb
     C                     KFLD           WQSR02           PD Producer Cod
     C                     KFLD           WGDZDT           PH Week Ending
      * Define keylist
     C           KRSSR     KLIST
     C                     KFLD           WQSR01           PH Company Numb
     C                     KFLD           WQSR02           PD Producer Cod
      * Setup key
     C                     Z-ADDWAHMNB    WQSR01           PH Company Numb
     C                     MOVELWAABCD    WQSR02           PD Producer Cod
     C                     Z-ADDWAAWDT    WGDZDT           PH Week Ending
      * Establish starting position
     C           KPSSR     SETLL@CGCPEJ                    *
     C           KRSSR     READE@CGCPEJ                  90*
      * Data record not found
     C   90                MOVEL'PRK0180' W0RTN   7
     C           *IN90     DOWEQ'0'
      * USER: Process Data record
      * First Time Processing
      * CASE: LCL.First Time Flag Usr is Yes
     C           YL0155    IFEQ 'Y'                        *IF
     C                     Z-ADDWGDZDT    YL0156           PH Week Ending
     C                     MOVEL'N'       YL0155           First Time Flag
     C                     END                             *FI
      * CASE: DB1.PH Week Ending Date NE LCL.PH Week Ending Date
     C           WGDZDT    IFNE YL0156                     *IF
     C                     GOTO SREXIT                     *QUIT
     C                     END                             *FI
      * CASE: DB1.PH Summary Type is 2 Week
     C           WGUVST    IFEQ '2WK'                      *IF
      * CASE: DB1.PH GA Head Killed is GE 600
     C           WGOWUI    IFGE 600                        *IF
      * PAR = DB1 By name
     C                     MOVELWGUVST    YL0145           PH Summary Type
     C                     Z-ADDWGORMB    YL0146           PH GA Avg Live
     C                     Z-ADDWGG9PC    YL0147           PH GA Adjusted
     C                     Z-ADDWGHBPC    YL0148           PH GA Avg Lean%
     C                     Z-ADDWGUWOE    YL0149           PH GA Avg Backf
     C                     Z-ADDWGHEPC    YL0150           PH GA Avg Loin
     C                     Z-ADDWGHGPC    YL0151           PH GA Avg Light
     C                     Z-ADDWGTIPR    YL0152           PH GA Lean Prm
     C                     Z-ADDWGB8A1    YL0153           PH GA Avg Srt D
     C                     MOVEL'Y'       YL0154           History Avail S
     C                     GOTO SREXIT                     *QUIT
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     ELSE
      * CASE: DB1.PH Summary Type is 4 Week
     C           WGUVST    IFEQ '4WK'                      *IF
      * CASE: DB1.PH GA Head Killed is GT Zero
     C           WGOWUI    IFGT 0                          *IF
      * PAR = DB1 By name
     C                     MOVELWGUVST    YL0145           PH Summary Type
     C                     Z-ADDWGORMB    YL0146           PH GA Avg Live
     C                     Z-ADDWGG9PC    YL0147           PH GA Adjusted
     C                     Z-ADDWGHBPC    YL0148           PH GA Avg Lean%
     C                     Z-ADDWGUWOE    YL0149           PH GA Avg Backf
     C                     Z-ADDWGHEPC    YL0150           PH GA Avg Loin
     C                     Z-ADDWGHGPC    YL0151           PH GA Avg Light
     C                     Z-ADDWGTIPR    YL0152           PH GA Lean Prm
     C                     Z-ADDWGB8A1    YL0153           PH GA Avg Srt D
     C                     MOVEL'Y'       YL0154           History Avail S
     C                     GOTO SREXIT                     *QUIT
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
     C                     END                             *FI
     C           KRSSR     READE@CGCPEJ                  90*
     C                     ENDDO
      *================================================================
     CSR         SREXIT    ENDSR
      /EJECT
